          (relu): ReLU(inplace=True)
        )
      )
      (avgpool): AdaptiveAvgPool2d(output_size=(1, 1))
      (flatten): Flatten()
    )
  )
  (heads): ModuleList(
    (0): MLP(
      (clf): Sequential(
        (0): Linear(in_features=2048, out_features=100, bias=True)
      )
    )
  )
)
